qemu-system-riscv64 \
	-machine virt \
	-kernel kernel-qemu \
	-m 1G \
	-nographic \
	-smp 1 \
	-bios default \
	-drive file=`pwd`/sdcard-rv.img,if=none,format=raw,id=x0 \
	-device virtio-blk-device,drive=x0,bus=virtio-mmio-bus.0 \
	-no-reboot \
	-device virtio-net-device,netdev=net \
	-netdev user,id=net \
	-rtc base=utc \
	-initrd initrd.img
